Our work extends directions taken in systems such as Ariane -LRB- Vauquois and Boitet , 1985 -RRB- , FoG -LRB- Kittredge and Polguere , 1991 -RRB- , JOYCE -LRB- Rambow and Korelsky , 1992 -RRB- , and LFS -LRB- Iordanskaja et al. , 1992 -RRB- .
